Turkish parliament speaker Omer_Izgi on Monday called an extraordinary parliamentary session for September 1 to vote on a proposal to hold early polls in November , NTV television reported . the move was initiated by the far-right Nationalist_Action_Party -lrb- MHP -rrb- , a partner in prime minister Bulent_Ecevit 's three-way governing coalition and now the biggest party in parliament . Ecevit has been under intense pressure to bring elections forward from April 2004 amid a deepening political turmoil in Turkey .
Egyptian president Hosni_Mubarak will meet with US secretary of state Warren_Christopher here on Sunday a day after Christopher announced the resumption of Israeli-Syrian peace talks , officials said . Christopher will brief Mubarak on the results of his talks with Syrian president Hafez_al-Assad and Israeli prime minister Shimon_Peres . the US secretary announced late Saturday that the negotiations would resume after a six-month freeze caused by a dispute over the future of the occupied Golan_Heights .

Clinton 's decisions are doomed to fail . '' .

Diouf said he planned an official visit to Mozambique as soon as possible . South_African un ambassador Dumisani_Kumalo requested the debate in a letter to Belinga-Eboutou written on behalf of the non-aligned nations movement . in it , Kumalo alluded to an earlier letter from the movement which `` emphasised the urgent need for a peaceful solution to the issue of Iraq . '' council members have for more than a month been considering the demand of the administration of US president George_W._Bush for a resolution defining tough new conditions for un weapons inspections in Iraq .

Argentina has issued an international arrest warrant for former president Carlos_Menem charging concealment of assets and money laundering , judicial sources said Wednesday . Menem , 73 , has been the subject of several Argentine investigations for corruption and arms trafficking since his 1989-1999 presidency . he faces arrest if he returns to Argentina , but has refused to do so . Menem , married to former Chilean miss universe Cecilia_Bolocco , lives in Chile , which has repeatedly refused to extradite him .

Italian archeologist Massimo_Pallottino , a specialist on Italy before the roman empire , has died at the age of 85 after a heart attack , it was reported Thursday . Pallottino , who died on Tuesday , was credited with inventing etruscology , having devoted his life to the study of the Etruscan people who lived north of Rome in pre-roman empire days . Pallottino 's 1964 discovery of Etruscan and Phoenician writings at Cerveteri north of Rome revolutionised the study of the people and their links with phoenicians , romans and carthaginians .
Filipino Mansueto_Velasco inflicted the first defeat on Cuba with a convincing points defeat over Yosvani_Aguilera in the second round of the light flyweight division at the olympics here Friday . Velasco downed Aguilera 14-5 , the Cubans ' first loss in 15 bouts . the victory puts Velasco into the quarter-finals and makes him a strong chance of fighting for the Philippines ' first boxing gold medal at an olympics .
Hungary approved Wednesday a US request to use a military base to train up to 3,000 Iraqi exiles , government spokesman Zoltan_Gal said . under the government decision , the United_States can train interpreters and other support personnel in Hungary 's southern Taszar base from January , Gal told a news conference . Gal said the training would include basic military techniques as well as interpreting skills , developing military-civilian ties and police skills . the Iraqi exiles being trained will be people who live either in the United_States or Europe , Gal said .

an advance team of nine US soldiers arrived in northeast Bosnia on Wednesday to carry out a reconnaissance of the area in preparation for the arrival of American ground troops . the team arrived in Tuzla by road from Kiseljak , west of Sarajevo , after bad weather prevented them flying into Tuzla airbase . `` i am here leading a small liason and transition team . we are doing the groundwork necessary to prepare for operations in this sector if a decision is made for us to operate in this area , '' colonel Joe_Brown , chief of staff of the first armoured division of the US_army , told reporters . '' under the deal , the two countries will create a joint military force and share aircraft carriers and nuclear test facilities .

Italian customs officials have seized 43 icons from a Russian traveller arriving at Rome airport , police said Saturday . Nikolai_Aguyev , 26 , was carrying the icons in his luggage and refused to explain to Italian police where they came from . experts from the Italian culture ministry confirmed the value and age of the icons . the ministry then proposed `` adopting '' the paintings exhibiting them in a museum . `` art smuggling is continual , we particularly look out for luggage from Russia and eastern European countries , '' a police spokesman said . `` in this case , we will hold an investigation to see if Aguyev was acting on his own or for a bigger organisation , '' the spokesman said .

Rump_Yugoslavia 's federal parliament is to vote on a new government in the near future after Yugoslav president Zoran_Lilic informed the speakers of its two chambers about his decision Saturday . legislative elections in Serbia and Montenegro -- Yugoslavia 's two republics -- were held on November 3 . Kontic , 59 , has been prime minister since March 2 , 1993 . Lilic decided on extending Kontic 's premiership after consulting with the leaders of the main parties represented in parliament .

Davoudi met Libyan leader Moamer_Kadhafi and other senior officials for discusssions that focused on economic cooperation and Iran 's nuclear programme , Libyan foreign minister Abdelrahman_Shalgham said . the accords covered the creation of a joint investment committee as well as cooperation in the fields of tourism , higher education , maritime transport and fishing , and an agreement between the two countries ' central banks , a Libyan official said .

Kremendahl was accused of accepting around 250,000 euros -lrb- dollars -rrb- worth of payments from a building magnate during a local election campaign in 1999 . the scandal had dogged the Social_Democrats and Schroeder during campaigning for the general election in September , which they won by a razor-thin margin .

Ciller will leave Ankara Sunday for Paris where she will attend ceremonies Monday before travelling to Moscow for further commemorations Tuesday . Turkey remained neutral throughout most of world war ii , but declared war on Germany in May 1945 , a few days before its end .

Polish president Aleksander_Kwasniewski said Saturday no particular country should be blamed for the failure of the EU summit in Brussels to reach an agreement on a constitution . `` it is impossible to put the responsibility for the absence of an agreement on one particular country , '' he told a news conference in Warsaw . the Brussels summit broke down after failing to bridge differences over voting rights in an enlarged EU , notably due to the refusal of Poland and Spain to surrender generous rights secured three years ago . Kwasniewski described the failure of the talks as an `` episode in the history of Europe . '' .

Arafat was dramatically air-lifted out of his West_Bank headquarters in Ramallah on Friday for emergency treatment in a French military hospital for a mystery blood disease .
Israel asked Peru on Tuesday to extradite a former Israeli official wanted on suspicion of taking bribes from Germany 's siemens company , judicial sources said . Dan_Cohen , a former manager of Israel 's electric company who also served as a district court judge , was arrested in Lima on Monday on a warrant , the sources said . Peru does not have an extradition treaty with Israel . Cohen fled Israel four years ago as suspicions emerged that he had pocketed about four million dollars , as part of a deal to purchase turbines manufactured by siemens he is also suspected of having fraudulently sold company real estate .

'' the play , a comedy which starts with a chance reunion between three old school friends , opened this week at the Bush_Theatre in west London , and runs until the end of June . Kokami himself is directing the production , billed as a `` quirky , wicked comedy . '' the play has enjoyed critical and commercial success in Japan since its premiere in 1993 . the playwright has brought his work to London in the past : in 1991 he directed a production of his play The_Angels with closed eyes at the mermaid Theatre .
an Australian court on Friday issued a landmark ruling that a quadriplegic man who wants to die had the right to stop being fed by his carers . Western_Australia 's chief judge Wayne_Martin said the Brightwater_Care_Group would not be criminally responsible if it ceased feeding and hydrating severely paralysed Christian_Rossiter , 49 , who had begged to be allowed to die . Martin said Rossiter had the right to direct his treatment , and food and water `` should not be administered against his wishes '' .

Medvedev said Russia objected to a handwritten addition made to the formal agreement by the Ukrainian side . `` i think that those who have signed this document with reservations well understand the legal consequences of their actions , '' he told Sergei_Lavrov . `` as a result , we are obliged to consider the document signed as null and void for us . we will not apply it as long as this reserve is not overturned , '' he added .

Bolani , himself a shiite , is an independent secular politician .

Orban 's three-party coalition has been in power since 1998 , when it succeeded a government led by the Socialist_Party , now the main opposition . Madl said the elections would allow the new government to get down to work as soon as possible on winding up negotiations on Hungary 's application to join the European_Union , which the country hopes to conclude by the end of 2002 .

Germany 's sickly economy was the main reason why half of all Germans gave up their summer holiday this year , according to the results of a survey released Wednesday . the poll of around 1,500 people found that financial worry was the biggest deterrent to a holiday , followed by job concerns . The_Iraq war , fears over the SARS virus and a summertime tiff between Italy and Germany , after an Italian minister said German tourists were arrogant , had little impact . favourite foreign destinations were Spain and Italy . one third of Germans spent their holidays at home , with the Baltic_Sea_coast the favourite destination .

Russian president Vladimir_Putin telephoned his US counterpart George_W._Bush on Monday to discuss Iraq and the Middle_East , the Kremlin said without disclosing further details . the Kremlin said in a statement that the call was made `` within the framework of regular consultations '' between the two leaders . Russia had opposed the us-led war in Iraq , coming to diplomatic blows with the United_States over the war and arguing for a greater role for the United_Nations in resolving the conflict .
CBS presenter Dan_Rather on Monday apologised on the network 's main evening news programme for the use of dubious documents to back a report casting doubt on president George_W._Bush 's military record . `` i want to say personally and directly , i 'm sorry , '' Rather said after highlighting the network 's regrets for using the documents which alleged that Bush had received preferential treatment to get into the Texas_Air_National_Guard . `` we can no long vouch for their authenticity , '' Rather said . `` it was a mistake . CBS_News deeply regrets it . '' CBS had issued a statement earlier in the day apologising for using the documents without fully checking their veracity .
French foreign minister Dominique_de_Villepin arrived in Kabul on Thursday for a brief visit which will include talks with president Hamid_Karzai . the French minister met the new special United_Nations representative for Afghanistan , Jean_Arnault , and was due to hold talks with Karzai and Afghan foreign minister Abdullah_Abdullah before heading to India .
US_Middle_East coordinator Dennis_Ross is to visit Egypt during a peace mission which he started on Monday in Israel , foreign minister Amr_Mussa said . Mussa said the mission aims to `` give a spark to the peace process on the Israeli-Syrian track . '' Ross was to meet Israeli foreign minister Ehud_Barak on Monday , before travelling to Syria and returning to the jewish state the next day for talks with prime minister Shimon_Peres . Peres is due in Cairo on Thursday to meet president Hosni_Mubarak .
unseeded frenchman Jo-Wilfried_Tsonga claimed the opening set 6-4 in the Australian open final against Serbian third seed Novak_Djokovic on Sunday . Tsonga had Djokovic 's serve under pressure after the pair exchanged service breaks in the opening two games . the frenchman broke the Serb again in the 10th game to take the first set in 49 minutes . it was the first set Djokovic has lost at the tournament .
US secretary of state Hillary_Clinton said Monday that North_Korea must repair ties with South_Korea before multilateral nuclear disarmament talks resume . `` this trilateral meeting reaffirmed the steps that North_Korea must take in order for a resumption of six-party talks , '' Clinton said at the end of a trilateral meeting with her counterparts from Japan and South_Korea . `` North_Korea must improve relations with the Republic_of_Korea and cease its provocative behavior , '' she said .
Chinese president Hu_Jintao said Friday the fundamentals of China 's economy had not changed , despite it facing difficulties and challenges due to the global financial crisis . `` the fundamentals of the Chinese economy have not changed . however , the global financial crisis has noticeably increased the uncertainties and factors for instability in China 's economic development , '' Hu said . `` we are now confronted with many difficulties and challenges in our economic endeavours , '' he said at the start of a gathering of Asian and European leaders in Beijing .
top seed Maria_Sharapova beat world number five Kim_Clijsters 6-4 , 6-2 Thursday to set up an Australian open final against Serena_Williams . there was no room for emotion as Sharapova clinically dispatched Clijsters in the Belgian 's final appearance at Melbourne_Park to become the first Russian woman ever to reach the tournament decider in Australia .
Israeli prime minister Ariel_Sharon told his weekly cabinet meeting Sunday he opposed a plan being drafted by foreign minister Shimon_Peres and Palestinian parliamentary speaker Ahmed_Qorei , officials in his office said . Sharon , who dismissed the plan when its outline first emerged in the press in December , said the propositions `` did not hold '' and told his ministers that he had said as much when he met Qorei Wednesday for the first time since becoming prime minister last March .
a military tribunal Tuesday formally charged general Yav_Nawej and colonel Eddy_Kapend with conspiracy and the murder of Democratic_Republic_of_Congo 's former president Laurent_Kabila . Kapend , the former head of the late president 's special staff , was arrested as a key suspect by Kinshasa authorities after Kabila was gunned down in his office on January 16 , 2001 . the president was shot by one of his bodyguards who was himself killed shortly after the assassination . state prosecutors later said that Kabila 's death was the outcome of a plot .
president Vladimir_Putin hailed an `` absolutely new quality '' in Russia 's partnership with the United_States during a summit meeting at the Kremlin with US leader George_W._Bush . `` today we are speaking about an absolutely new quality of our relationship , regarding questions of security , questions of reducing our strategic potentials and creating a new secure world , '' Putin said after one-on-one talks with Bush .
Turkey on Monday called back its ambassador from Libya for consultations after sharp criticism by Libyan leader Moamer_Kadhafi , a statement issued by the foreign ministry here said . at a joint press conference Saturday during a controversial three-day trip to Libya by Turkish prime minister Necmettin_Erbakan , Kadhafi had described Turkey as a `` country under western occupation since the end of world war ii . '' .
Nikolai_Korbut was named Wednesday head of the Belarus central bank , the ITAR-TASS_news_agency reported . Korbut , who was previously vice-president of the bank , replaced president Tamara_Vinnikova , who was fired Tuesday by a decree of Belarus president Alexander_Lukashenko . Vinnikova is suspected of abusing her power and embezzlement while in a prior job as president of the commercial bank Belarus , according to Belarus_interior_ministry officials cited by Interfax_agency .
Japan will build a refugee camp in Croatia , where some four million people have been displaced by ethnic strife in the former Yugoslavia , foreign minister Yohei_Kono was quoted as saying Wednesday . Kono disclosed the plan at a meeting here with UN_High_Commissioner_for_Refugees Sadako_Ogata , Kyodo_News_Service said . the Japanese foreign minister will officially announce the project when he visits Croatia from Friday to Sunday , it said .
United_States envoy James_Kelly left China Thursday morning after holding one-day talks with Chinese officials on the North_Korean nuclear crisis . Kelly , Washington 's top diplomat for Asia , arrived in Beijing from Seoul Tuesday night and met officials , including Chinese vice foreign minister Li_Zhaoxing , on Wednesday . the visit was part of a flurry of diplomatic efforts to bring the three-month-long crisis over Pyongyang 's plans to restart its nuclear program to an end . Kelly is headed to Singapore and from there to Indonesia and Japan .
German chancellor Helmut_Kohl and French president Jacques_Chirac expressed confidence Wednesday that their countries will meet the conditions required to qualify for European monetary union in 1999 . speaking a joint press conference after talks here , Kohl rejected a proposal by six leading German economic institutes that the conditions , which concern issues including public debt and budget deficits , be eased . Chirac for his part said `` together we will be ready to meet the international and monetary deadlines that we have undertaken . '' .
Peruvian government lawyers called Friday for Chile to place Peru 's ex-president Alberto_Fujimori under house arrest ahead of a Supreme_Court ruling on his extradition , a judicial source told AFP . the request sent to the Chilean_Supreme_Court prosecutor cited the `` gravity '' of the charges against him . Fujimori has been free to move about in Chile while awaiting the country 's decision on whether to extradite him to Peru where he faces charges of corruption and human rights violations during during his 1990-2000 presidency .
British_Defense secretary Michael_Portillo arrived Saturday in Saudi_Arabia where he is to discuss weapons purchase and other military issues with Saudi leaders , an official said . Saudia_Arabia is one of Britain 's primary clients for weapons , with contracts worth billions of dollars . Britain is hoping to win a one billion dollar contract for the sale of 150 tanks to the Saudi army , the British official said . Portillo is to meet his Saudi counterpart , Prince_Sultan_ibn_Abdel_Aziz , during the visit .
Russia must develop offensive weapons systems to counter US missile defence plans , prime minister Vladimir_Putin was quoted by Russian news agencies as saying on Tuesday . `` to preserve the balance , we must develop offensive weapons systems , not missiles defence systems as the United_States is doing , '' Putin was quoted as saying on a working visit to Russia 's Far_East . `` the problems of missile defence and offensive arms are very closely linked , '' Putin added , quoted by ITAR-TASS . `` by building such an umbrella over themselves our -lrb- US -rrb- partners could feel themselves fully secure and will do whatever they want , which upsets the balance . '' .
-lrb- by Sofia wu -rrb- president Chen_Shui-bian said Thursday that a balanced relationship between the two sides of the Taiwan_Strait is the key to the formation of a `` new peaceful pacific order . '' Chen made the remarks at a news conference introducing the soon-to-be-inaugurated Democratic_Pacific_Union -lrb- DPU -rrb- , which was conceived by vice president Annette_Lu to boost cooperation among Pacific_Rim democracies . in his keynote speech , Chen said he is convinced that only a normalized , constructive cross-strait relationship based on the principles of parity and pragmatism can sustain Asia-Pacific prosperity and advancement .
the new commander of the southern Israel military region , which includes the Gaza_Strip , took up his post Monday , a military statement said . a ceremony , which saw outgoing commander general Doron_Almog hand over to general Dan_Harel , took place in Tel_Aviv and was attended by defense minister Shaul_Mofaz and the army 's chief of staff general Moshe_Yaalon , the statement said . according to Israeli media reports , Almog is being considered as a senior aide to Yaalon .

the US ambassador to France , Pamela_Harriman , has paid tribute to former French president Francois_Mitterrand , who died Monday , saying the United_States had `` lost a great friend '' and France a great man . she said international affairs for decades to come would be stamped by his personality and commitment to European unity .
the violence that broke out in Port-au-Prince on Friday is unacceptable , the US embassy spokesman here said Friday . the attack by pro-military junta groups on a march by supporters of exiled president Jean-Bertrand_Aristide had been made possible by `` inadequate Haitian police protection on the streets , '' resulting in `` several deaths and a number of injuries , '' Stanley_Schrager told reporters . `` this behavior is unacceptable , '' Schrager said . but Schrager congratulated the organisers of the demonstration which commemorated the third anniversary of the coup which overthrew Aristide in September 1991 .
Palestinian prime minister Ahmed_Qorei and his emergency cabinet were officially sworn in Tuesday by Yasser_Arafat in a ceremony at the Palestinian leader 's headquarters here . Qorei and six of the eight other members of the cabinet pledged `` to be faithful to the law of the country and the interests of the Palestinian people . '' Arafat declared Qorei as prime minister in a decree late Sunday in which he also announced a state of emergency . incoming interior minister Nasser_Yussuf and minister without portfolio Jawad_Tibi were unable to attend the brief ceremony .
austrian Andreas_Goldberger became the ski jump world champion for the first time here on Sunday winning his 19th World_Cup event in the process . Goldberger lay second overnight to Finland 's Janne_Ahonen , but his two jumps of 194 and 198 metres were godd enough to give him the title . Ahonen finished second and Slovenia 's urban franc was third . the biggest loser was Germany 's Christophe_Duffner who slipped from second overnight to fifth .
Spain and Morocco said Tuesday they had stepped up anti-terror cooperation in the Strait_of_Gibraltar in response to a heightened security alert in the two countries . Spanish foreign minister Miguel_Angel_Moratinos and his Moroccan counterpart taieb Farsi fihri made the announcement at a joint news conference in Madrid . Morocco had Friday raised its terrorism alert to the maximum level to indicate a `` current threat '' against the north African country , the interior ministry said .
tottenham striker Jermain_Defoe has been axed by Martin_Jol for Sunday 's crucial Premier_League clash at bolton . Defoe , 24 , scored twice after coming off the bench in Thursday 's UEFA cup win over Anorthosis_Famagusta , but spurs boss Jol has opted to travel to the reebok stadium without the England international . German prosecutors said Friday that two senior Rwandan_Hutu rebel leaders , Ignace_Murwanashyaka and Straton_Musoni , have been indicted on charges of crimes against humanity and war crimes . Murwanashyaka , political leader of the Democratic_Forces_for_the_Liberation_of_Rwanda -lrb- FDLR -rrb- , and his deputy Musoni were arrested in November 2009 . the FDLR has been accused of atrocities in eastern Democratic_Republic_of_Congo since fleeing Rwanda after the 1994 genocide .
Japanese prime minister Ryutaro_Hashimoto said Monday he was closely watching the Russian presidential election in which incumbent Boris_Yeltsin was fighting a close race with Gennady_Zyuganov . `` Yeltsin previously had a large lead but some opinion polls just before the vote indicate his narrower lead . Japan is watching the final result , '' Hashimoto was quoted as telling reporters , without further comment . chief cabinet secretary Seiroku_Kajiyama told a press conference that Japan hoped the Russian drive for reforms would continue . `` the free and fair elections show the progress in Russian democracy , '' Kajiyama said .
Pakistani opposition leader Benazir_Bhutto called on the international community to stop backing Pervez_Musharraf , telling AFP Tuesday it was time for him to quit as president and army chief . `` general Musharraf must quit . he must quit as president and as chief of army staff , '' she said in a telephone interview from house arrest in the eastern city of Lahore . `` i call on the interntaional community to stop backing him , to stop backing the man whose dictatorship threatens to engulf this nuclear-armed state in chaos , '' Bhutto added .
German chancellor Angela_Merkel condemned on Thursday the murder of Russian rights campaigner Natalya_Estemirova , saying the killing in the Caucasus must be investigated . `` i think that on the Russian side , everything must be done to catch the killer , '' Merkel said after talks with Russian president Dmitry_Medvedev in Munich . Estemirova , 50 , was found dead on Wednesday afternoon in Ingushetia with gunshot wounds to the head and chest hours after being seen bundled into a car outside her home in the Chechen capital Grozny .

'' .

German chancellor Gerhard_Schroeder said Sunday that he was `` encouraged '' by the results obtained in Iraq by chief un weapons inspector Hans_Blix . `` we are encouraged by the news that we have received '' after Blix 's visit , Schroeder said at a press conference in Berlin with Russian president Vladimir_Putin . `` we have to find out if Iraq has weapons of mass destruction or not , '' he said , adding that to do that , the inspectors would need more time .
the Canadian government confirmed Monday that it has contingency plans to evacuate its citizens from Hong_Kong in case of civil unrest there . but Foreign_Ministry spokesman Geoffrey_Chapman said newspaper reports of the evacuation plan in both Canada and Hong_Kong had been `` exaggerated , to say the least . '' he said Canada maintained such contingency plans for its citizens in about 112 countries , including Hong_Kong , and that there had been no recent changes in the Hong_Kong plan . Chapman insisted Ottawa anticipated a peaceful transition next year from British rule to Chinese sovereignty of the territory .

Belarus police on Monday released an Agence_France-Presse -lrb- AFP -rrb- journalist after arresting her in the wake of mass nighttime rallies against the re-election of president Alexander_Lukashenko . Maria_Antonova was arrested as she tried to return to her hotel after the rallies were broken up by the police in the early hours of Monday morning . after spending the night in detention , Antonova was released Monday afternoon , without being given an explanation for her arrest . Belarus police arrested hundreds of protestors , including seven opposition candidates , after smashing the mass rally protesting fraud in the landslide re - election of Lukashenko .

Paris_Saint_Germain 's Guerin last played in February last year in a 1-0 friendly win in Italy , while the last appearance of Bordeaux 's Zidane was on October 8 against Romania .

intelligence that Iran had a nuclear weapons programme that was halted in 2003 `` validates '' US pressure on Tehran 's nuclear policy , US_Defence secretary Robert_Gates said Tuesday . `` if anything the new national estimates validate the administration 's strategy to bring diplomatic and economic pressure on the Iranian government 's nuclear policy , '' Gates said during a visit to Afghanistan . a US_National_Intelligence_Estimate released on Monday said that Iran halted its nuclear weapons drive in 2003 .
Spanish prime minister Jose_Maria_Aznar said Saturday he remains opposed to proposed changes to EU voting rights included in a draft EU constitution . along with incoming EU member Poland , Spain is holding out to keep the voting rights it secured under the 2000 Nice_Treaty , which give both countries 27 votes against 29 for Germany , which is twice the size . `` there is no consensus on this issue . we are going to maintain this position , '' Aznar told reporters after the first session of talks aimed at finalizing the EU 's first ever constitution by December .
`` all indications '' are that Irish voters have rejected the EU_Lisbon_Treaty in a referendum , European_Commission chief Jose_Manuel_Barroso said Friday . `` all indications are that Ireland has voted no to the treaty of Lisbon , '' Barroso told journalists in Brussels . `` as a supporter of the treaty , the European_Commission would have hoped for another result . however , we respect the outcome of the referendum . '' .
Iranian president Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad on Wednesday started a news conference in which he was expected to address the row with Britain over its arrested sailors and Iran 's nuclear programme . the conference , which was being shown live on Iranian television , marks the start of the Iranian new year on March 21 and is the president 's fifth such meeting with reporters since taking office . the event started with the reading of verses from the Koran on islamic unity as Ahmadinejad , dressed in a light suit , sat solemnly behind a desk and a picture of a mosque .

Choate is a political economist who has been campaigning with the Texas billionaire who is running on the Reform_Party ticket for the November 5 vote . he was a staunch opponent of the North_American_Free_Trade_Agreement and advocates a tough line against Japan 's trade policies . Perot had kept his pick close to his chest , saying he would announce his decision Tuesday live on a prime-time television `` infomercial '' followed by an interview with the running mate on CNN .

the case of Ulrike_Maier , who died in a World_Cup skiing race last year , is being reopened with lawyer Steffen_Ufer filing for `` involuntary homicide '' against course organisers . Ufer is representing the relatives of Maier , who died of head injuries after falling and colliding with a timing post during a downhill race at Garmisch-Partenkirchen on January 29 1994 . course organisers denied negligence and Munich prosecutors stopped their investigation in October 1994 . the 1989 and 1991 super giant slalom champion , aged 26 , left a daughter melanie and partner Heinrich_Schweighofer .

a woman who hired a hit man to kill her husband 's lover got more than she bargained for when the assassin murdered her instead , state media reported Monday . the Beijing woman agreed to pay Li_Changjiang 100,000 yuan -lrb- 12,100 US dollars -rrb- to kill or disfigure her husband 's mistress but when he failed to do so she demanded the money back . Li , with associates Zhang_Hongyu and Sun_Yanhai , showed they had no qualms about carrying out the deadly deed by killing her instead , the xinhua news agency said . the Beijing first intermediate people 's court sentenced Li to death Friday and he was executed Monday . Sun was sentenced to life imprisonment while Zhang remains at large .

'' Putin had earlier hit out at Ukraine for delivering weapons used by Georgia to fight Russia during a brief conflict in August .

Sharon , who met earlier with US secretary of state Colin_Powell , was scheduled to meet at the White_House Tuesday with president George_W._Bush .
Guatemalan president Alfonso_Portillo will pay a state visit to Taiwan from April 6-12 , hoping to achieve closer bilateral ties , his spokesman said Tuesday . `` president Portillo is travelling at the invitation of the government of Taiwan . one of the objectives is to boost trade and our political relationship , because Guatemala , like the rest of Central_America , has sought greater space in the international community on Taiwan 's behalf , '' spokesman Byron_Barrera said . Barrera said the Guatemalan delegation would be small and that its expenses would be paid for by Taipei .
Iran arrested on Monday several aides to reformist ex-president Mohammad_Khatami and opposition leader Mir_Hossein_Mousavi , an opposition website reported . Khatami aides `` Morteza_Haji and -lrb- hasan -rrb- rasooli were arrested , '' Parlemannews said . the two men run Khatami 's non-governmental baran organisation . `` Mousavi advisors Alireza_Beheshti , -lrb- ghorban -rrb- behzadian-nejad and -lrb- Mohammad -rrb- bagherian were also arrested in the morning , '' it added . the arrests signal an increased crackdown on the opposition .
Taiwan 's top police official Chang_Shih-liang has resigned over the pre-election shooting of president Chen_Shui-bian , an official said Monday . National_Police_Agency spokesman huang tsung-jen told AFP that Chang `` had tendered his resignation to premier Yu_Shyi-kun Friday night to take responsibility for the shooting of president Chen . '' the premier has yet to say whether the resignation has been accepted .
Russian president Boris_Yeltsin and his US counterpart Bill_Clinton held a `` very lively '' telephone conversation on enlarging NATO , Yeltsin was quoted as saying by interfax on Saturday . the conversation , which took place on Friday on Clinton 's initiative , lasted 40 minutes and Clinton promised to carefully consider Russian objections to NATO 's proposed enlargement to include Moscow 's former allies in eastern Europe , the news agency said . Yeltsin said he was sending Washington a `` serious message '' on the matter .

'' the US president has ordered an end to US combat operations in Iraq by August 31 2010 , but says 50,000 troops will remain under a new mission until the end of 2011 .

Jones will take over the role on a date still to be determined , a NATO statement said . `` the president -lrb- of the United_States -rrb- asked the member governments to agree to release General_Ralston from his assignment . having been asked to nominate a successor , the president proposed general Jones , '' a NATO statement said . Ralston has been in the job , traditionally always filled by a member of the US_army , since May 2000 .
US president George_W._Bush is to name Mike_Johanns , governor of the Midwestern state of Nebraska , to replace Ann_Veneman as agriculture secretary , a White_House official said Thursday . the president would announce the appointment later in the day , the official said . Johanns , a republican , was elected Nebraska governor in 1998 and was re-elected to the post in 2002 . Veneman , the first woman to hold the post of US secretary of agriculture , submitted her resignation following Bush 's November 2 re-election .

Kyrgyzstan 's interim government could use force against ousted president Kurmanbek_Bakiyev if he tries to destabilise the country , interim official Omurbek_Tekebayev said Sunday on Kyrgyz radio . `` the interim government is prepared to use force in the event that Bakiyev attempts to destabilise the situation , '' Tekebayev said . Bakiyev fled the capital Bishkek on Wednesday amid massive protests against his rule . interim Kyrgyz leader Roza_Otunbayeva has accused Bakiyev , who is now located in the south of the country , of attempting to foment civil war .
Egyptian president Hosni_Mubarak arrived in China Wednesday at the start of a four-day state visit , official Chinese media said . Mubarak touched down in Beijing to begin a trip which will see him hold talks with president Jiang_Zemin and other Chinese leaders , the xinhua news agency reported . the talks will be aimed at strengthening cooperation between the countries as well as discussing international and regional issues , the report said .
Georgian president Mikhail_Saakashvili was set to visit Ukraine on Friday following opposition leader Viktor_Yushchenko 's weekend victory in presidential elections there , the presidential office here said . an official confirmed the trip but gave no further details . the meeting comes after west-leaning Yushchenko 's so-called `` orange revolution '' forced a rerun of an earlier rigged presidential ballot claimed by his rival , Viktor_Yanukovich . us-educated Saakashvili was elected in January on the back of a similar popular movement dubbed the `` rose revolution '' . both Georgia and Ukraine were constituent republics of the former Soviet_Union until its collapse in 1991 .
US president George_W._Bush has freed up to 15 million dollars to meet `` unexpected urgent refugee and migration needs '' in the event of a war against Iraq , the White_House announced Thursday . `` such an emergency may arise if it becomes necessary for the United_States and other nations to use military force to disarm the Iraqi regime of its weapons of mass destruction , '' Bush said in a memorandum dated Wednesday . the monies may go to international , government , and nongovernmental organizations that work with refugees , according to the memorandum , which the White_House released .
France and Japan signed a deal Monday aimed at improving the safety of a new generation of fast-breeder nuclear reactors , officials said Monday . the deal , signed by French and Japanese nuclear authorities , aims to complete studies into accidents which could lead to a partial or total meltdown in such reactors . the accord was signed by the French nuclear safety body IPSN , French power company Electricite_de_France and the Japan 's Power_Reactor_and_Nuclear_Fuel_Development_Corporation .
a contingent of 30 Australian_Federal_Police officers will be sent to Haiti to help the United_Nations restore law and order , foreign minister Gareth_Evans said Wednesday . Evans said the team would spend up to six months in the Caribbean country to monitor how Haitian police performed their duties . the police will be part of a un-sanctioned multinational force which will also include police from Argentina , Bangladesh , Belgium , Britain and the Netherlands .
Greece and Turkey concluded an agreement overnight acknowledging Greek sovereignty over a disputed Aegean islet , following the intervention of US assistant secretary of state Richard_Holbrooke , Greek_Defence minister Gerassimos_Arsenis said Wednesday . the accord enabled both Turkish and Greek forces to disengage from around Imia , or Kardak , a rocky islet off Turkey 's southwest coast whose possession is the object of a dispute that flared at the weekend between Athens and Ankara .
Japanese trade minister Ryutaro_Hashimoto is to propose at the forthcoming APEC meeting in Indonesia that Japan host a conference on energy-related issues in the Asia-Pacific region next April . the joint government-private sector conference would deal with ways to improve supply-demand relations as the region is likely to face an energy shortage if economies continue to expand at the current pace , Hashimoto told reporters . Hashimoto met the press before the ministerial meeting of the Asia - Pacific_Economic_Cooperation -lrb- APEC -rrb- forum in Jakarta starting November 6 .

Rudolf_Scharping , head of the Social_Democrat -lrb- SPD -rrb- group in the German lower house the bundestag , was seriously injured in the head on Thursday in a cycling accident , Koblenz police said . an SPD spokeswoman in Bonn said the first medical examinations showed Scharping was suffering from concussion . she could not say how long he would be hospitalized . Scharping , who was not wearing a helmet , fell off his bicycle after braking too sharply on a slope near attenhausen in western Germany not far from lahnstein where he lives . he was taken by helicopter to a hospital here .

Two Italian engineers were kidnapped and their driver was killed Wednesday in an area of southwest Colombia where leftist guerrillas are active , the Italian news agency ANSA reported . initial reports said the italians had not been injured . the kidnapping occurred in the southwest department of santander . the agency said the italians were working on an oil project for the Italian firm TPL , one of Italy 's largest construction and engineering companies . the men , Salvatore_Rossi , 55 , and Giuliano_Ponzanelli , 47 , were abducted while driving to the santander airport . leftist guerrillas have been fighting successive Colombian governments for decades .

The_United_States and Cuba reached an agreement Friday aimed at stemming the exodus of Cuban refugees at sea , the White_House said . the agreement was reached during discussions in New_York between Cuban and US negotiators , said officials traveling with president Bill_Clinton . the accord calls for the legal immigration of at least 20,000 Cubans into the United_States each year . under the agreement , Cuba pledges to `` to take effective measures to prevent the unsafe departure of Cubans , '' said a White_House statement . there was no immediate announcement from the Cuban side .

Russian journalists have frequently come under attack , and last month the chief editor of the Togliatti observer , in the city of Togliatti in the Volga region , Alexei_Sidorov , was stabbed to death outside his home . investigators said the killing was a purely criminal affair , but Russian media disputed this version . Sidorov 's predecessor was murdered in similar circumstances in April 2002 .

Egyptian president Hosni_Mubarak asked Egypt 's parliament on Saturday to amend the constitution to allow for direct , multiparty presidential elections this year for the first time in the nation 's history . some opposition politicians and analysts hailed the proposal as heralding a new political era for Egypt , the Arab_world 's most populous nation , while skeptics said they wanted to await the details to be sure that the eventual constitutional amendment would not create only the appearance of democracy , a common problem in the region .

Battisti , 52 , disappeared in August 2004 , shortly before the French government signed an extradition order to return him to Italy , where he has been convicted in absentia for four murders . a former member of the armed proletarians for communism , Battisti lived in Paris from 1990 and made his name as a crime writer .

Mexican president Felipe_Calderon announced that he would fly on Tuesday to visit the southern Mexican region ravaged by Hurricane_Dean . the powerful category five storm uprooted trees and tore down power lines across the Yucatan_Peninsula on its way to the oil-rich Gulf_of_Mexico after slamming onto Mexico 's Caribbean coast . Calderon was in Montebello at a two-day summit with the leaders of Canada and the United_States .

Sugar complained to the fa after last weekend 's Sunday_Mirror story in which Ruddock , who was sold by spurs to liverpool in 1993 , was quoted as saying : `` Sugar is not running spurs as a football club . his meanness has dragged spurs down . '' .

New_York_State attorney general Elliot_Spitzer announced Monday an inquiry into mutual fund sales by investment bank Morgan_Stanley . the probe will investigate whether Morgan_Stanley improperly pressured brokers and branch managers to sell mutual funds to investors who were not made aware that their brokers received additional compensation for pitching in-house funds . Morgan_Stanley is also alleged to have misled regulators investigating the practice . Spitzer announced the probe in Boston together with Massachusetts secretary of state William_Galvin . `` this is a legitimate and important inquiry , of vital importance to millions of investors who buy mutual funds from their brokers , '' Galvin told reporters .

former US president Bill_Clinton and US journalists Euna_Lee and Laura_Ling returned Wednesday from North_Korea , one day after North_Korea 's leader Kim_Jong-Il pardoned the two women . their chartered aircraft landed at 1250 gmt , and was taxiing into a hangar where the party was to address the media . US_TV journalist Lisa_Ling was seen entering the plane which brought her sister Laura , whom she calls her best friend , home from the ordeal which began back in March . both women are married and Lee has a young daughter she has not seen since leaving on assignment .
Japan Olympic_Committee -lrb- joc -rrb- honorary chairman Katsuji_Shibata died of pulmonary emphysema at a Tokyo hospital Saturday , doctors said . he was 83 . Shibata , who became joc honorary chairman in 1989 after serving as chairman since 1977 , led Japanese teams to the 1972 Sapporo winter olympics in Japan , the Los_Angeles olympics in 1984 and the Seoul olympics in 1988 .

German cement maker HeidelbergCement said Wednesday it planned to cut 470 jobs at its Dutch and Belgian units , enci and CBR , where it is encountering difficulties . `` market developments , ie . the increase in cement imports into Belgium and the Netherlands , led to a noticeable drop in sales at CBR and enci in recent years , '' HeidelbergCement said in a statement . the company would therefore embark on a restructuring of its production capacity in those countries , `` which could lead to a reduction in the headcount by approximately 200 jobs in Belgium and 270 jobs in the Netherlands , '' the statement said .
Pakistan 's two major opposition leaders signed a formal declaration Sunday on forming a coalition government , and urged president Pervez_Musharraf to convene parliament without delay . Asif_Ali_Zardari , widowed husband of ex-premier Benazir_Bhutto , and Nawaz_Sharif signed the agreement at a news conference here after a fresh round of coalition talks following last month 's general election . Zardari is the de facto leader of Bhutto 's Pakistan people 's party , which won the most seats in the February 18 ballot and , along with Sharif 's party , trounced Musharraf 's political allies .

Cheney will serve as acting president until such time as Bush , who will be under anesthesia , says he is ready to resume his duties , presidential spokesman Tony_Snow told reporters . `` the president has had no symptoms '' of cancer , said Snow , who noted that Bush had been scheduled for such an examination since undergoing a colonoscopy in June 2002 .

'' .

Gates said the reductions in December were the start of a US military transition in Iraq that will leave a long-term presence in Iraq at `` a fraction of the size of today 's desployed force . '' `` all the president 's senior military commanders and advisers are in agreement with what general Petraeus has recommended and what the president has approved , '' he said .

The_United_States has offered to open discussions on a new START_III arms reduction treaty , vice president Al_Gore said Friday . `` we have started discussions about the possibility that we could together create guidelines for what start III could accomplish , '' Gore said in a joint press conference with Russian prime minister Viktor_Chernomyrdin . the START ii treaty was ratified last year by the US_Congress , but has been held up in the Russia_Duma where some oppose the pact which calls for slashing strategic nuclear warheads on both sides to no more than 3,500 by 2003 .
the Italian authorities have decided to extradite to the United_States Monya_Elson , whom US police suspect of being one of the heads of the Russian mafia , judicial sources here said Wednesday . Elson , arrested one year ago in central Italy , will be flown to New_York on August 22 . he is expected to face charges on several counts of murder , attempted murder , gun running and drugs offences . he does not however run the risk of receiving the death sentence , since capital punishment was only reintroduced in the state where he lived after he committed the alleged crimes . in Italy he was wanted for money laundering through an import company he had set up in the Adriatic resort of fano .

McCain has vowed to unmask Obama as a radical sympathizer at the debate , as he has slipped further in the polls ahead of the November 4 presidential elections . ahead of the evening debate at Hofstra_University on Long_Island , the New_York_Daily_News tabloid ran a front-page caricature of a gun-toting McCain emerging from a wild west bar , under the headline `` last chance saloon . '' .

'' .

Jedynka and other radio stations also fell silent for 60 seconds . over the weekend , Polish president Aleksander_Kwasniewski sent a message to Russian counterpart , Vladimir_Putin , expressing `` deep shock at the barbarous act of terrorism '' , while many poles lit candles outside the Russian embassy here and Russian consulates in memory of the victims .

Savchenko and Szolkowy , who have been skating together since 2003 , are the reigning two-time world pairs champions and have won the European crown for the last three years .

Soederberg and Lagerbaeck led Sweden to the 2002 World_Cup finals in Korea and Japan this summer without a single defeat and the new contract shows the faith showed in them by the nation 's football officials . the country 's federation said in a statement the new deal would mean the coaches , the team and Swedish football , would be able to work with peace of mind .

the war crimes trial of former Macedonian interior minster Ljube_Boskovski and his former bodyguard , Johan_Tarculoski , will start April 16 , according to documents released on Wednesday by the United_Nations_court in The_Hague . Boskovski and Tarculoski have been in custody since March 2005 at the facilities of the un tribunal for the former Yugoslavia . they are accused of war crimes against ethnic albanians during an uprising in 2001 , including the alleged murder of seven people in the village of Ljuboten near Skopje . the two men are the only Macedonians to have been brought before the un tribunal since its creation in 1993 .

'' Germany , along with other members of the European_Union and signators to the European_Convention_on_Human_Rights , rejects capital punishment . `` it is a position of principle , '' Schroeder told the Bild_am_Sonntag newspaper . `` it is applicable to all -- including a dictator like Saddam_Hussein , even if he has behaved in an execrable way toward others . '' Schroeder , a Social_Democrat , was a leading opponent of the us-led invasion of Iraq .

'' he added that Washington `` knew from the beginning '' that Iran `` was not seeking to obtain the atomic bomb . '' .

'' the strike in which 23 other people were wounded was claimed by the radical hamas movement . Straw urged the Palestinian_Authority to meet its security obligations and Israel to show restraint .
former US vice president Spiro_Agnew , who served under president Richard_Nixon from 1969-1973 , has died at a Maryland hospital , Cable_News_Network said Wednesday . he was 77 . the former Maryland governor was taken to a hospital in Ocean_City , Maryland , where he passed away Tuesday , CNN said , adding that no other details about his death were released . officials at Ocean_City 's Atlantic General_Hospital would not confirm or deny the report . Agnew resigned as vice president while facing charges of tax evasion in 1973 , one year before Nixon was brought down by the watergate scandal .

Germany and France have had summits every six months since 1963 , with the site alternating between the two nations . additional summits are generally held each time the French president or Germany chancellor is changed . Chirac has , however , already met with German chancellor Helmut_Kohl on May 18 , shortly after Chirac was sworn in .

Tehran rejects the Arab-Israeli peace process as a sell-out of moslem rights , whereas Amman signed a peace treaty with Israel in October 1994 .

Issa_Salomi , 60 , became unaccounted for on January 23 and was believed to have been kidnapped by a shiite militant group in Baghdad , where he was assigned to US forces . Salomi , an interpreter for the US_army , was returned on March 25 , the department said Saturday , adding the circumstances of his disappearance were under investigation .

'' .

Robson said : `` i am interested in quality players and Barmby fits into that category . but i am not interested in a reported price tag of seven million pounds . i think someone has plucked that figure out of the air . '' .

South_Africa 's parliament passed a motion Wednesday condemning France 's resumption of nuclear testing in the South_Pacific . The_National_Assembly adopted the motion that slammed `` France 's blatant disregard for international opinion '' and called on the government of France to stop nuclear testing immediately . all parties supported the motion , although the formerly-ruling National_Party called for the motion to be extended to condemn China 's nuclear test programme . this amendment was rejected . the South_African government has previously released statements expressing concern over both French and Chinese nuclear tests .

former US vice president Dick_Cheney , who has a long history of heart problems , was hospitalized Monday after experiencing chest pains , his office said . the controversial republican figure was `` resting comfortably '' at George_Washington_University_Hospital in the US capital and his doctors were evaluating the situation , his office said in a statement . Cheney , who has had four heart attacks and had a pacemaker installed in his chest in 2001 , was scheduled to meet with former president George_W._Bush and other staffers from the Bush administration in Washington on Friday for the first time since they left office last January .
International_Monetary_Fund chief Rodrigo_Rato expressed confidence Thursday in the World_Bank 's ability to resolve a nepotism controversy swirling around its president , Paul_Wolfowitz . `` i have total confidence in the institution , '' Rato told reporters when asked about the path ahead in the damaging row that has engulfed the IMF 's sister organization . Wolfowitz is accused of favoritism over hefty pay rises given to his girlfriend at the development lender . earlier Thursday the former deputy US_defense secretary apologized for a `` mistake '' over the employment terms of libyan-born Shaha_Riza , but refused to say if he might quit as the World_Bank board met to debate the matter .
Wales will have a new skipper for the November 6 test match against Australia in the shape of scarlets hooker Matthew_Rees . Rees , who has won 39 caps , will takes over from ospreys back-row forward Ryan_Jones who needs time to fully recover from a calf muscle tear sustained while playing for his region against Glasgow last Sunday . Jones will be reassessed after the Australia clash to determine when he might be able to return . his injury is the latest setback to hit the Wales camp after full-back Lee_Byrne was ruled out of the first three autumn tests due to a broken bone in his hand .
Russian lawmakers should ratify a major nuclear disarmament treaty with the United_States , president Vladimir_Putin said on Saturday , news agencies reported . `` Russia wants to see this document ratified . we will work with deputies of the chambers of parliament and i hope that we will move to ratification , '' Putin was quoted as saying . Russian ratification of the so-called `` Moscow treaty '' had been scheduled for late last month , but the State_Duma lower house of parliament called off the vote in protest at the us-led war in Iraq .
Hungarian defence minister Gyorgy_Keleti and army chief of staff Janos_Deak left for Trondheim , Norway , Saturday , to watch NATO 's large-scale strong resolve military exercises , MTI news agency said . the exercises will be carried out by 22,000 new fast Reaction_Force troops from 16 North_Atlantic_Treaty_Organisation states . during a four-day Norway visit , Keleti is expected to meet Norwegian defence minister Jorgen_Kosmo .
chancellor Angela_Merkel thanked Americans for their support as the Berlin_Wall fell 20 years ago , telling the US_Congress in a rare address Tuesday that Germany would never forget the US help . `` ladies and gentlemen , to put it in just one sentence , i know , we Germans know , how much we owe to you our American friends . and we shall never , i personally shall never , ever forget this , '' Merkel said .
Pope_John_Paul_II held a private meeting with former Polish president Lech_Walesa on Monday , a Vatican spokesman said . he added that the meeting was informal and `` very friendly . '' announcing the meeting several days ago , Andrzej_Zakrzewski , a close advisor to walesa , said that walesa wanted to `` thank the Pope for his spiritual and moral support '' of his native Poland and wished to discuss `` some Polish issues '' with the pontiff . after his talks with walesa , the Pope met with walesa 's wife Danuta_Walesa , as well as the Polish ambassador to the Holy_See and with the former president 's advisors .
Palestinian president Mahmud_Abbas , on a visit to Amman , Wednesday welcomed the appointment of Tony_Blair as special envoy for the diplomatic quartet pushing for Middle_East peace , an official said . `` president Abbas welcomes the nomination of mr Blair as envoy of the quartet , '' chief Palestinian negotiator Saeb_Erakat told AFP . `` the president , who was consulted on the matter , has given the assurance that he will work with mr Blair to arrive at a peaceful solution on the basis of two states , '' he added .
president Bill_Clinton on Saturday nominated investment banker James_Wolfensohn as the next president of the World_Bank to succeed ailing president Lewis_Preston . Clinton said in a statement he will ask the bank 's board of directors to confirm the nomination of Wolfensohn , 61 , who has served as chairman of the John_F._Kennedy_Center_for_the_Performing_Arts in Washington since 1990 .
Russia launched its photon sattelite with Russian , French and European experiments aboard , from the Plessetsk space centre in northern Russia , ITAR-Tass_news_agency said Friday , monitored here . the satellite was blasted into space with a soyuz rocket late Thursday and will remain in orbit for 15 days , the agency said . the sattelite , which is due to come down in the Kazakhstan steppes early next month , carries five Russian experiments into the fusion and study of materials in space , and two studies into cellular biology for France and the European_Space_Agency .
Branko_Ivankovic was named on Tuesday new coach of Croatian league and cup champions Dynamo_Zagreb , the club said . Ivankovic signed for four years , replacing zvonimir soldo , who resigned last week after four months in the club . media speculated that the club 's sports director Zoran_Mamic and his brother Zdravko , the club 's vice-president , were not satisfied with soldo 's independent way of working . Ivankovic , 54 , has already been dynamo 's coach from 2006 until January when he resigned over a row with Zdravko_Mamic .
rebels from Burundi 's last remaining hutu insurgent group , the National_Liberation_Forces -lrb- FNL -rrb- , on Wednesday gave the head of the Catholic_Bishops_Conference , Simon_Ntamwana , 30 days to leave the country . the warning comes after Ntamwana accused the rebels of murdering the Vatican 's ambassador to Burundi , Michael_Courtney . Courtney was killed in an ambush on Monday , and Ntamwana said the rebels were responsible , describing the attack as `` a real execution . '' .
Greek foreign minister George_Papandreou could travel to Baghdad as part of efforts to defuse the Iraq crisis if the rest of the EU agrees , his spokesman said Monday . `` foreign minister Papandreou has said that he would be ready under certain conditions to go even to Baghdad , '' Panayotis_Beglitis told AFP on the sidelines of an EU foreign ministers ' meeting in Brussels . Greece currently holds the rotating EU presidency .
Scotland , represented by Colin_Montgomerie and Marc_Warren , won the World_Cup for the first time here on Sunday defeating the United_States in a play-off for the title . the scots won on the third extra hole after they had finished the tournament level on 25 under par with Americans Heath_Slocum and Boo_Weekley . the win was all the sweeter for Montgomerie and Warren as they lost out in a play-off last year to Germany in Barbados . the French pairing of Raphael_Jacquelin and Gregory_Havret were third on 24 under par .
a German veterinarian working for a European_Union -lrb- EU -rrb- project who was taken hostage in northern Somalia last month has been released after 19 days in captivity , the EU_office here announced Thursday . Heinz_Stachelscheid who was working in the sanaag region of Somalia for the German non-governmental organisation johanniter was freed unconditionally on Monday after mediation by Somali elders . no reasons were given for the abduction . Stachelscheid travelled to Djibouti for a medical check-up before returning to Germany .
The_European_Commission offered Wednesday to help Spain and Morocco settle a territorial dispute after Madrid sent troops to evict Moroccan soldiers from a tiny Mediterranean_island . its president Romano_Prodi said the commission -- the EU 's administrative arm -- was ready to `` facilitate dialogue '' between two countries in their dispute over the uninhabited islet of Perejil just off the coast of Morocco . earlier Wednesday , elite Spanish troops ousted about a dozen Moroccan soldiers sent to Perejil a week ago in what Rabat said was a measure against terrorism and illegal immigration .
German chancellor Angela_Merkel and a party in her conservative alliance have agreed to accept the resignation of economy minister Michael_Glos , party sources told AFP . sources close to the leadership of the Christian_Social_Union -lrb- CSU -rrb- , the Bavarian sister party to Merkel 's Christian_Democrats , said party chief Horst_Seehofer had reached an accord with the chancellor on Glos leaving the cabinet . Glos had asked Seehofer Saturday to be relieved of his post but the CSU leader rejected the bid , saying the minister still had his full confidence .
China has refused to hand over five North_Koreans it detained from a Japanese consulate in northeast China to Japan despite repeated requests , a Japanese diplomat said Tuesday . `` they said they can not do that because there is no international or domestic legal basis for that , '' the diplomat said , following a two - hour meeting between Masaaki_Ono , chief of the Japanese foreign ministry 's consular and immigration department , and his Chinese counterpart in Beijing .
the Polish border guard on Monday arrested 20 kurds from Turkey and one Iraqi as they tried to enter Poland illegally from Ukraine , a spokesman said . border spokesman Witold_Jodlowski said the people in question were planning to go from Poland illegally into the European_Union and would now be returned to the Ukraine . they also arrested two poles awaiting the immigrants and three suspected Ukrainian traffickers , he said .
Iraqi president Jalal_Talabani denied on Wednesday Turkish reports that he had offered to extradite leaders of the rebel Kurdistan_Workers ' party -lrb- PKK -rrb- based inside Iraq . `` we have said several times that the leaders of the PKK do not stay in kurdish cities of Iraq but they live with thousands of their fighters in the Qandil_mountains . it is impossible to arrest them and deliver them to Turkey , '' said a statement issued by the office of Talabani , who is himself a kurd .
US president George_W._Bush left Thursday for a tour of Latin_America and a week of meetings aimed at promoting democracy and free trade . Bush will also work to convince his regional counterparts to reject what his administration calls the `` false promises '' of leftist leaders , such as Venezuela 's Hugo_Chavez , who advocate an alternative world vision . the president will make his first stop in Brazil before heading to Uruguay , Colombia , Guatemala and Mexico . Chavez is marking Bush 's trip with a parallel tour .
French president Nicolas_Sarkozy has commissioned former socialist foreign minister Hubert_Vedrine to draw up a report on globalisation , Vedrine said Tuesday . Vedrine , who was foreign minister from 1997 to 2002 , has been asked to produce `` concrete proposals '' about how to promote French and European interests `` in this new globalised world '' . Sarkozy , who took office in May , has appointed a number of socialist politicians to his government , including foreign minister Bernard_Kouchner and European_Affairs minister Jean-Pierre_Jouyet .
rangers manager Walter_Smith announced on Saturday that his former England striker Mark_Hateley will move to Queens_Park_Rangers for one million pounds on Monday . `` we have agreed a fee with Queens_Park_Rangers for Mark_Hateley and they wish to parade him before Monday 's game with spurs , '' said Smith . Hateley , who will be 34 in November , has scored more than 100 goals in five years with the Scottish champions and cost one million pounds from French club Monaco in 1990 .
the first suspected case in Russia of the killer pneumonia that has hit around the world has been recorded after a Russian flew in from China with similar symptoms , interfax reported on Friday . a Russian sailor who arrived on a flight from the Chinese city of Harbin on Friday at the pacific port city of Vladivostok has been quarantined , the region 's deputy chief medical officer Lyudmilla_Grebenkova told the news agency .
US president George_W._Bush will meet with New_Zealand 's prime minister Helen_Clark late next month for talks on the fight against terrorism , the White_House said Wednesday . Bush will host Clark at the White_House on March 21 , the White_House said in a statement . `` president Bush looks forward to consulting with prime minister Clark on common efforts in the war on terror , '' the statement said . the two will also discuss ways to strengthen bilateral ties .
Germany 's Tony_Martin , riding for the htc-columbia team , won the Eneco_Tour cycling race on Tuesday after claiming the seventh and final stage . Martin won the final 16.9 km time-trial ahead of Dutch rider Maarten_Tjallingi and dane Alex_Rasmussen . in the final standings Martin took the title ahead of Koos_Moerenhout of the Netherlands and Norway 's Edvald_Boasson_Hagen .
Qatar 's appeal court Monday upheld the death sentence handed down against a Jordanian journalist for spying . judge Abdullah_Saadi rejected the appeal by Firas_Majali , an employee of Qatari state television and son of a former Jordanian information minister . the death sentence is subject to the approval of Qatar 's emir . Majali was condemned to death by Qatar 's supreme court on October 22 after being convicted of spying for a `` foreign country '' widely identified as Jordan .
un secretary-general Kofi_Annan appointed British diplomat Ralph_Zacklin as the temporary replacement for Jose_Ayala_Lasso of Ecuador as high commissioner for human rights , a un spokesman said here on Wednesday . Lasso is leaving his UN_post on March 15 to become Ecuador 's foreign minister , spokesman Juan_Carlos_Brandt said . Zacklin , the number two in the United_Nations ' legal affairs department , will serve as high commissioner until a permanent successor is named , Brandt said .
Vladimir_Shumeiko , chairman of the upper house of Russia 's parliament , began Monday a four-day trip to Israel during which he will prepare for the first visit by foreign minister Andrei_Kozyrev . officials said Shumeiko would meet prime minister Yitzhak_Rabin and foreign minister Shimon_Peres on Tuesday . Kozyrev whose country co-sponsors the Middle_East peace process with the United_States is expected to visit Israel in early April , a foreign ministry spokesman said .
Russian and western negotiators have failed to reach agreement over Russian participation in a multi-national peacekeeping force for former Yugoslavia , US trouble-shooter Richard_Holbrooke said Tuesday . the question of Russian participation in this force is `` not yet fully resolved , '' he told reporters following a meeting of the `` contact group '' of Britain , France , Germany , Russia and the United_States in Moscow . Russia has refused to allow its troops to take part in a force which would be under the command of the North_Atlantic_Treaty_Organisation , as envisaged by the west .
US_Senate republicans elected Bill_Frist as their leader Monday , his office said . the 51 republican members of the senate elected Frist in a telephone conference call , a staffer in his Washington office said . president George_W._Bush , who is close to Frist , was quick to congratulate the incoming republican leader . `` senator Frist has earned the trust and respect of his colleagues on both sides of the aisle . `` i look forward to working with him and all members of the senate and house to advance our agenda for a safer , stronger and better America , '' Bush said in a statement .
Japan 's injury woes worsened at the World_Cup on Friday with the news that both centre Shotaro_Onishi and flanker Yasunori_Watanabe would be unable to play again . coach John_Kirwan said that both men picked up serious injuries in the 72-18 loss to Wales here on Thursday night . Kirwan said that Onishi had suffered a popped rib cartilage and would be out of action for three to four weeks . Watanabe suffered a suspected detached bicep and will undergo scans on Friday evening to confirm the full extent of the injury .
a former New_Orleans police officer and a hit man have been sentenced to death for conspiring to murder a woman who filed a civil rights complaint against the officer , the US_Justice_Department announced Wednesday . a jury in New_Orleans convicted former officer Len_Davis of violating federal criminal civil rights laws by hiring Paul_Hardy to murder kim marie groves , a New_Orleans woman . groves had filed a civil rights complaint against Davis and his partner , Sammie_Williams . groves had complained to the police department that Davis and Williams had beaten a young man without provocation , prompting Davis to hire hit-man Hardy to kill her . the murder occurred in October 1994 .
millwall chief Mick_McCarthy is the new manager of the Republic_of_Ireland football squad , taking over from Jack_Charlton . his appointment to the post , speculated in the British press , was confirmed on Monday by millwall chairman Peter_Mead . Charlton , whose reign came to an end when Ireland failed to qualify for this year 's European_Championships , had recommended McCarthy for the job . McCarthy was born in England , but played 57 times for the republic -- captaining the side at the 1990 World_Cup finals in Italy and earning his last cap against Portugal in 1992 .
Taiwan premier Yu_Shyi-kun Friday offered to send delegates to rival China for talks . Yu told a press conference shortly after he was inaugurated as the island 's new premier that he welcomed recent ouvertures by Chinese leaders towards Taiwan . `` we , therefore , consider sending related people to visit the mainland , and exchange views on issues of mutural concern , '' he said . `` we are glad to see communist Chinese authorities have become pragmatic to face the reality that the Democratic_Progressive_Party is the ruling party '' on the island . Beijing and Taipei were split in 1949 at the end of a bitter civil war .

German chancellor Gerhard_Schroeder expressed doubt Friday that military action against Iraq could be avoided , in an interview with NTV television . `` can a war be avoided ? i have doubts that we will be able to stop one . but i refuse to give in to those doubts , '' Schroeder said . he affirmed that Germany wanted un weapons inspectors to continue their work verifying president Saddam_Hussein 's assertions that Iraq has no weapons of mass destruction programme .

a former Canadian olympic light heavyweight boxer has been sentenced to three years for assault and robbery . Brent_Kosolofski , 30 , pleaded guilty to breaking into an apartment in September 1993 with another man whose identity is not known . they grabbed the tenant at gunpoint , beat him and demanded to know where certain drugs were stashed , the court was told . but Kosolofski fell asleep at the apartment , allowing the victim to escape . when Kosolofski realized what had happened , he jumped from the third floor window to a parking lot , breaking his pelvic bone . Kosolofski , a member of Canada 's 1988 olympic team in Seoul , is originally from Calgary in Alberta .
Top_Taliban and al-qaeda members are being hunted in Pakistan as the extremist groups are no longer primarily based in Afghanistan , the US special envoy to Afghanistan , Zalmay_Khalilzad , said Wednesday . `` Afghanistan is no longer the principal base for the al-qaeda , but i think there are figures near and across the border in Pakistan , '' he told reporters in New_Delhi . `` we know there are several top Taliban leaders in Pakistan and we would like them arrested and turned over to afghani authorities . certainly there are remnants of the al-qaeda in Pakistan , '' Khalilzad said .
Belgian former world number one Kim_Clijsters was set to marry American basketball star Brian_Lynch in a civil court later Thursday , ahead of the religious ceremony on Saturday in her home town of bree . since her retirement from the sport in May , Clijsters has been living with Lynch in Belgium . `` everyone is welcome at the civil ceremony , '' revealed the town 's mayor , Jaak_Gabriels , in the flemish newspaper hat laatste nieuws . the Belgian ace , who won 34 WTA singles titles in her career including the US_Open in 2005 , said that battling injuries and the constant effort to stay at the top had finally taken their toll and it was time to hang up her racket .
a Belgian doctor who has worked for a decade on aids research was named Monday to head a new un program set up to coordinate efforts to fight the virus that causes the disease . the appointment of Peter_Piot to head the program was announced by un secretary-general Boutros_Boutros-Ghali , who said the aids virus could be contained if action were taken `` as a world community . '' Piot , 45 , is a former professor of microbiology at the Institute_of_Tropical_Medicine in the Antwerp , Belgium , and has served since 1992 as the deputy director of the World_Health_Organization anti-aids program .
the health of paramount Chinese leader Deng_Xiaoping is improving , Chinese prime minister Li_Peng has told Indonesia 's president suharto , the official Antara news agency said Sunday . the comments were made in Copenhagen where Li and suharto are attending the un world social development summit . no other details about the ailing Chinese patriarch 's health were included . Indonesian state secretary murdiono said Li also told suharto that the Deng succession in China would proceed `` normally '' because the process of changing the leadership has already been well formed , Antara reported .
Uganda 's president Yoweri_Kaguta_Museveni will visit Japan from September 7-11 to hold talks with prime minister Tomiichi_Murayama , the foreign ministry said Tuesday . Museveni and his wife , Janet_Kataaha , would also meet Japanese emperor akihito and empress michiko during their visit , the ministry said . they are also scheduled to visit Osaka and Kyoto in western Japan , it said .
